class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eDasar Teori\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-dasar-teori\" class=\"anchor\" 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDalam Single Linked List, setiap node menyimpan data dan pointer yang menunjuk ke node berikutnya dalam urutan sekuensial. Berikut adalah ilustrasi yang memperbaiki konsep Single Linked List:\nrust\nCopy code\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+\n|  1  | -----\u0026gt; |  2  | -----\u0026gt; |  3  | -----\u0026gt; |  4  | -----\u0026gt; NULL\n+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+\n| data|        | data|        | data|        | data|\n| next| -----\u0026gt; | next| -----\u0026gt; | next| -----\u0026gt; | next|\n+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePada ilustrasi di atas, terdapat empat node yang saling terhubung membentuk Single Linked List. Setiap node memiliki dua bagian utama, yaitu data (nilai yang disimpan) dan next (pointer yang menunjukkan ke node berikutnya). Node terakhir memiliki pointer next yang menunjuk ke NULL, menandakan akhir dari Single Linked List.\nNode pertama memiliki data dengan nilai 1 dan next yang menunjuk ke node kedua. Node kedua memiliki data dengan nilai 2 dan next yang menunjuk ke node ketiga. Node ketiga memiliki data dengan nilai 3 dan next yang menunjuk ke node keempat. Node keempat memiliki data dengan nilai 4 dan next yang menunjuk ke NULL.\nDengan menggunakan struktur seperti ini, Single Linked List memungkinkan penyimpanan dan pengelolaan data dalam urutan sekuensial dengan fleksibilitas yang tinggi, karena node-node dapat ditambahkan atau dihapus secara dinamis.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDouble Linked List Circular adalah jenis dari struktur data Linked List di mana setiap node memiliki tiga bidang (field): satu bidang pointer yang menunjuk ke node berikutnya (next), satu bidang pointer yang menunjuk ke node sebelumnya (prev), dan satu bidang untuk menyimpan data yang sesuai untuk node tersebut.\nPada Double Linked List Circular, pointer next dan prev pada node terakhir di list akan menunjuk kembali ke node pertama, membentuk sebuah lingkaran atau siklus. Hal ini memungkinkan navigasi data dalam kedua arah (maju dan mundur) secara efisien dan dengan mudah, karena setiap node memiliki akses ke node sebelumnya dan node berikutnya.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eGuided\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-guided\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Guided\" href=\"#guided\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e1. 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include \u0026lt;iostream\u0026gt;\nusing namespace std;\n\n/// PROGRAM SINGLE LINKED LIST NON-CIRCULAR\n// Deklarasi Struct Node\nstruct Node\n{\n    // komponen/member\n    int data;\n    Node *next;\n};\nNode *head;\nNode *tail;\n// Inisialisasi Node\nvoid init()\n{\n    head = NULL;\n    tail = NULL;\n}\n// Pengecekan\nbool isEmpty()\n{\n    if (head == NULL)\n        return true;\n    else\n        return false;\n}\n// Tambah Depan\nvoid insertDepan(int nilai)\n{\n    // Buat Node baru\n    Node *baru = new Node;\n    baru-\u0026gt;data = nilai;\n    baru-\u0026gt;next = NULL;\n    if (isEmpty() == true)\n    {\n        head = tail = baru;\n        tail-\u0026gt;next = NULL;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        baru-\u0026gt;next = head;\n        head = baru;\n    }\n}\n// Tambah Belakang\nvoid insertBelakang(int nilai)\n{\n    // Buat Node baru\n    Node *baru = new Node;\n    baru-\u0026gt;data = nilai;\n    baru-\u0026gt;next = NULL;\n    if (isEmpty() == true)\n    {\n        head = tail = baru;\n        tail-\u0026gt;next = NULL;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        tail-\u0026gt;next = baru;\n        tail = baru;\n    }\n}\n// Hitung Jumlah List\nint hitungList()\n{\n    Node *hitung;\n    hitung = head;\n    int jumlah = 0;\n    while (hitung != NULL)\n    {\n        jumlah++;\n        hitung = hitung-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n    return jumlah;\n}\n// Tambah Tengah\nvoid insertTengah(int data, int posisi)\n{\n    if (posisi \u0026lt; 1 || posisi \u0026gt; hitungList())\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi diluar jangkauan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n    else if (posisi == 1)\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        Node *baru, *bantu;\n        baru = new Node();\n        baru-\u0026gt;data = data;\n        // tranversing\n        bantu = head;\n        int nomor = 1;\n        while (nomor \u0026lt; posisi - 1)\n        {\n            bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n            nomor++;\n        }\n        baru-\u0026gt;next = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n        bantu-\u0026gt;next = baru;\n    }\n}\n// Hapus Depan\nvoid hapusDepan()\n{\n    Node *hapus;\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        if (head-\u0026gt;next != NULL)\n        {\n            hapus = head;\n            head = head-\u0026gt;next;\n            delete hapus;\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            head = tail = NULL;\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n// Hapus Belakang\nvoid hapusBelakang()\n{\n    Node *hapus;\n    Node *bantu;\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        if (head != tail)\n        {\n            hapus = tail;\n            bantu = head;\n            while (bantu-\u0026gt;next != tail)\n            {\n                bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n            }\n            tail = bantu;\n            tail-\u0026gt;next = NULL;\n            delete hapus;\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            head = tail = NULL;\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n// Hapus Tengah\nvoid hapusTengah(int posisi)\n{\n    Node *hapus, *bantu, *bantu2;\n    if (posisi \u0026lt; 1 || posisi \u0026gt; hitungList())\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi di luar jangkauan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n    else if (posisi == 1)\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        int nomor = 1;\n        bantu = head;\n        while (nomor \u0026lt;= posisi)\n        {\n            if (nomor == posisi - 1)\n            {\n                bantu2 = bantu;\n            }\n            if (nomor == posisi)\n            {\n                hapus = bantu;\n            }\n            bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n            nomor++;\n        }\n        bantu2-\u0026gt;next = bantu;\n        delete hapus;\n    }\n}\n// Ubah Depan\nvoid ubahDepan(int data)\n{\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        head-\u0026gt;data = data;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List masih kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n// Ubah Tengah\nvoid ubahTengah(int data, int posisi)\n{\n    Node *bantu;\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        if (posisi \u0026lt; 1 || posisi \u0026gt; hitungList())\n        {\n            cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi di luar jangkauan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        }\n        else if (posisi == 1)\n        {\n            cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            bantu = head;\n            int nomor = 1;\n            while (nomor \u0026lt; posisi)\n            {\n                bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n                nomor++;\n            }\n            bantu-\u0026gt;data = data;\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List masih kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n// Ubah Belakang\nvoid ubahBelakang(int data)\n{\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        tail-\u0026gt;data = data;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List masih kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n// Hapus List\nvoid clearList()\n{\n    Node *bantu, *hapus;\n    bantu = head;\n    while (bantu != NULL)\n    {\n        hapus = bantu;\n        bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n        delete hapus;\n    }\n    head = tail = NULL;\n    cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List berhasil terhapus!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n}\n// Tampilkan List\nvoid tampil()\n{\n    Node *bantu;\n    bantu = head;\n    if (isEmpty() == false)\n    {\n        while (bantu != NULL)\n        {\n            cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; bantu-\u0026gt;data \u0026lt;\u0026lt; ends;\n            bantu = bantu-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;List masih kosong!\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\nint main()\n{\n    init();\n    insertDepan(3);\n    tampil();\n    insertBelakang(5);\n    tampil();\n    insertDepan(2);\n    tampil();\n    insertDepan(1);\n    tampil();\n    hapusDepan();\n    tampil();    hapusBelakang();\n    tampil();\n    insertTengah(7, 2);\n    tampil();\n    hapusTengah(2);\n    tampil();\n    ubahDepan(1);\n    tampil();\n    ubahBelakang(8);\n    tampil();\n    ubahTengah(11, 2);\n    tampil();\n    return 0;\n}\n\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e#\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003estruct\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eNode\u003c/span\u003e\n{\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e//\u003c/span\u003e class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e;\n}\n\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFungsi-fungsi ini memungkinkan pengguna untuk mengelola linked list sesuai dengan kebutuhan, baik itu menambahkan, menghapus, mengubah data, atau membersihkan seluruh isi list. Program juga memberikan feedback kepada pengguna jika terjadi kesalahan seperti menambahkan node di posisi yang tidak valid atau mengubah node yang tidak ada. Program berjalan secara interaktif, memberikan menu pilihan kepada pengguna untuk memilih operasi yang ingin dilakukan pada linked list.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e2. data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include \u0026lt;iostream\u0026gt;\nusing namespace std;\n\n\nclass Node {\n    public:int data;\n    Node* prev;\n    Node* next;\n};\nclass DoublyLinkedList {\n        public:\n        Node* head;\n        Node* tail;\n        DoublyLinkedList() {\n            head = nullptr;\n            tail = nullptr;\n    }\n    void push(int data) {\n        Node* newNode = new Node;\n        newNode-\u0026gt;data = data;\n        newNode-\u0026gt;prev = nullptr;\n        newNode-\u0026gt;next = head;\n        if (head != nullptr) {\n            head-\u0026gt;prev = newNode;\n        } \n        else {\n            tail = newNode;\n        }\n        head = newNode;\n    }\n    void pop() {\n        if (head == nullptr) {\n            return;\n        }\n        Node* temp = head;\n        head = head-\u0026gt;next;\n        if (head != nullptr) {\n            head-\u0026gt;prev = nullptr;\n        } \n        else {\n            tail = nullptr;\n        }\n        delete temp;\n    }\n    bool update(int oldData, int newData) {\n        Node* current = head;while (current != nullptr) {\n            if (current-\u0026gt;data == oldData) {\n                current-\u0026gt;data = newData;\n                return true;\n            }\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n    void deleteAll() {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            Node* temp = current;\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            delete temp;\n        }\n        head = nullptr;\n        tail = nullptr;\n    }\n    void display() {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; current-\u0026gt;data \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot; \u0026quot;;\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n};\n\n\nint main() {\n    DoublyLinkedList list;\n    while (true) {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;1. Add data\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;2. Delete data\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;3. Update data\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;4. Clear data\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;5. Display data\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;6. Exit\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;int choice;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Enter your choice: \u0026quot;;\n        cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; choice;\n        switch (choice) {\n            case 1: {\n                int data;\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Enter data to add: \u0026quot;;\n                cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; data;\n                list.push(data);\n                break;\n            }\n            case 2: {\n                list.pop();\n                break;\n            }\n            case 3: {\n                int oldData, newData;\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Enter old data: \u0026quot;;\n                cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; oldData;\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Enter new data: \u0026quot;;\n                cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; newData;\n                bool updated = list.update(oldData, newData);\n                if (!updated) {\n                    cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Data not found\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            case 4: {\n                list.deleteAll();\n                break;\n            }\n            case 5: {\n                list.display();\n                break;\n            }\n            case 6: {\n                return 0;\n            }\n            default: {\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Invalid choice\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e#\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003einclude\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\u0026lt;\u003c/span\u003eiostream\u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eData not found\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n                }\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ebreak\u003c/span\u003e;\n            }\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ecase\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e4\u003c/span\u003e: {\n                list.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003edeleteAll\u003c/span\u003e();\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ebreak\u003c/span\u003e;\n            }\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ecase\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e5\u003c/span\u003e: {\n                list.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003edisplay\u003c/span\u003e();\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ebreak\u003c/span\u003e;\n            }\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ecase\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e6\u003c/span\u003e: {\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e;\n            }\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edefault\u003c/span\u003e: {\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eInvalid choice\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ebreak\u003c/span\u003e;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e;\n}\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eKode yang Anda berikan adalah implementasi dari sebuah program yang menggunakan Double Linked List untuk mengelola data. Program ini memberikan menu interaktif kepada pengguna untuk melakukan operasi-operasi dasar pada Double Linked List, seperti menambah data, menghapus data, mengubah data, membersihkan seluruh data, dan menampilkan data.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eUnguided\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-unguided\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Unguided\" href=\"#unguided\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e1. Soal mengenai Single Linked List\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-1-soal-mengenai-single-linked-list\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 1. Lakukan operasi berikut:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#include \u0026lt;iostream\u0026gt;\n#include \u0026lt;string\u0026gt;\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Deklarasi Struct Node\nstruct Node {\n    string nama;\n    int usia;\n    Node* next;\n};\n\n// Inisialisasi Node\nNode* head = nullptr;\n\n// Pengecekan List Kosong\nbool isEmpty() {\n    return head == nullptr;\n}\n\n// Tambah Node di Depan\nvoid insertDepan(string nama, int usia) {\n    Node* newNode = new Node;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;nama = nama;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;usia = usia;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;next = head;\n    head = newNode;\n}\n\n// Tambah Node di Belakang\nvoid insertBelakang(string nama, int usia) {\n    Node* newNode = new Node;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;nama = nama;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;usia = usia;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;next = nullptr;\n    \n    if (isEmpty()) {\n        head = newNode;\n        return;\n    }\n\n    Node* current = head;\n    while (current-\u0026gt;next != nullptr) {\n        current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n    current-\u0026gt;next = newNode;\n}\n\n// Tambah Node di Tengah\nvoid insertTengah(string nama, int usia, string posisi) {\n    Node* current = head;\n    while (current != nullptr \u0026amp;\u0026amp; current-\u0026gt;nama != posisi) {\n        current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n\n    if (current == nullptr) {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Posisi tidak ditemukan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        return;\n    }\n\n    Node* newNode = new Node;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;nama = nama;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;usia = usia;\n    newNode-\u0026gt;next = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    current-\u0026gt;next = newNode;\n}\n\n// Hapus Node dengan Nama Tertentu\nvoid hapus(string targetNama) {\n    Node* current = head;\n    Node* prev = nullptr;\n\n    while (current != nullptr \u0026amp;\u0026amp; current-\u0026gt;nama != targetNama) {\n        prev = current;\n        current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n\n    if (current == nullptr) {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Data tidak ditemukan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        return;\n    }\n\n    if (prev == nullptr) {\n        head = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    } else {\n        prev-\u0026gt;next = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n\n    delete current;\n}\n\n// Ubah Data Node dengan Nama Tertentu\nvoid ubahData(string targetNama, string newNama, int newUsia) {\n    Node* current = head;\n    while (current != nullptr \u0026amp;\u0026amp; current-\u0026gt;nama != targetNama) {\n        current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n    if (current != nullptr) {\n        current-\u0026gt;nama = newNama;\n        current-\u0026gt;usia = newUsia;\n    } else {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Data tidak ditemukan\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    }\n}\n\n// Tampilkan Seluruh Data\nvoid tampilkanData() {\n    Node* current = head;\n    while (current != nullptr) {\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; current-\u0026gt;nama \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot; \u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; current-\u0026gt;usia \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string namaAnda;\n    int usiaAnda;\n    cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Masukkan Nama Anda: \u0026quot;;\n    cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; namaAnda;\n    cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Masukkan Usia Anda: \u0026quot;;\n    cin \u0026gt;\u0026gt; usiaAnda;\n\n    insertDepan(namaAnda, usiaAnda);\n\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;John\u0026quot;, 19);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Jane\u0026quot;, 20);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Michael\u0026quot;, 18);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Yusuke\u0026quot;, 19);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Akechi\u0026quot;, 20);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Hoshino\u0026quot;, 18);\n    insertBelakang(\u0026quot;Karin\u0026quot;, 18);\n\n    hapus(\u0026quot;Akechi\u0026quot;);\n    insertTengah(\u0026quot;Futaba\u0026quot;, 18, \u0026quot;John\u0026quot;);\n    insertDepan(\u0026quot;Igor\u0026quot;, 20);\n    ubahData(\u0026quot;Michael\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;Reyn\u0026quot;, 18);\n\n    cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Data Mahasiswa:\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n    tampilkanData();\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e#\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003einclude\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan DoublyLinkedList() {\n        head = nullptr;\n    }\n\n    void tambah_data(string nama_produk, int harga) {\n        Node* new_node = new Node(nama_produk, harga);\n        if (head == nullptr) {\n            head = new_node;\n        } else {\n            Node* current = head;\n            while (current-\u0026gt;next != nullptr) {\n                current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            }\n            current-\u0026gt;next = new_node;\n            new_node-\u0026gt;prev = current;\n        }\n    }\n\n    void hapus_data(string nama_produk) {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            if (current-\u0026gt;nama_produk == nama_produk) {\n                if (current-\u0026gt;prev != nullptr) {\n                    current-\u0026gt;prev-\u0026gt;next = current-\u0026gt;next;\n                }\n                if (current-\u0026gt;next != nullptr) {\n                    current-\u0026gt;next-\u0026gt;prev = current-\u0026gt;prev;\n                }\n                if (current == head) {\n                    head = current-\u0026gt;next;\n                }\n                delete current;\n                return;\n            }\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n    }\n\n    void update_data(string nama_produk, int harga) {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            if (current-\u0026gt;nama_produk == nama_produk) {\n                current-\u0026gt;harga = harga;\n                return;\n            }\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n    }\n\n    void tambah_data_urutan_tertentu(string nama_produk, int harga, int urutan) {\n        Node* new_node = new Node(nama_produk, harga);\n        if (urutan == 1 || head == nullptr) {\n            new_node-\u0026gt;next = head;\n            if (head != nullptr) {\n                head-\u0026gt;prev = new_node;\n            }\n            head = new_node;\n        } else {\n            Node* current = head;\n            int count = 1;\n            while (current != nullptr \u0026amp;\u0026amp; count \u0026lt; urutan - 1) {\n                current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n                count++;\n            }\n            if (current == nullptr) {\n                cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Urutan melebihi jumlah produk yang ada\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n                return;\n            }\n            new_node-\u0026gt;next = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            new_node-\u0026gt;prev = current;\n            if (current-\u0026gt;next != nullptr) {\n                current-\u0026gt;next-\u0026gt;prev = new_node;\n            }\n            current-\u0026gt;next = new_node;\n        }\n    }\n\n    void hapus_data_urutan_tertentu(int urutan) {\n        if (head == nullptr) {\n            return;\n        }\n        Node* current = head;\n        if (urutan == 1) {\n            head = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            if (head != nullptr) {\n                head-\u0026gt;prev = nullptr;\n            }\n            delete current;\n            return;\n        }\n        int count = 1;\n        while (current != nullptr \u0026amp;\u0026amp; count \u0026lt; urutan) {\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            count++;\n        }\n        if (current == nullptr) {\n            return;\n        }\n        if (current-\u0026gt;next != nullptr) {\n            current-\u0026gt;next-\u0026gt;prev = current-\u0026gt;prev;\n        }\n        if (current-\u0026gt;prev != nullptr) {\n            current-\u0026gt;prev-\u0026gt;next = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n        delete current;\n    }\n\n    void hapus_seluruh_data() {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            Node* next_node = current-\u0026gt;next;\n            delete current;\n            current = next_node;\n        }\n        head = nullptr;\n    }\n\n    void tampilkan_data() {\n        Node* current = head;\n        cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot;Nama Produk Harga\u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n        while (current != nullptr) {\n            cout \u0026lt;\u0026lt; current-\u0026gt;nama_produk \u0026lt;\u0026lt; \u0026quot; \u0026quot; \u0026lt;\u0026lt; current-\u0026gt;harga \u0026lt;\u0026lt; endl;\n            current = current-\u0026gt;next;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    DoublyLinkedList dll;\n\n    // Menambahkan data awal\n    dll.tambah_data(\u0026quot;Originote\u0026quot;, 60000);\n    dll.tambah_data(\u0026quot;Somethinc\u0026quot;, 150000);\n    dll.tambah_data(\u0026quot;Skintific\u0026quot;, 100000);\n    dll.tambah_data(\u0026quot;Wardah\u0026quot;, 50000);\n    dll.tambah_data(\u0026quot;Hanasui\u0026quot;, 30000);\n\n    // Modifikasi sesuai dengan case yang diberikan\n    dll.tambah_data_urutan_tertentu(\u0026quot;Azarine\u0026quot;, 65000, 3);\n <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dasar Teori</h2><a id="user-content-dasar-teori" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dasar Teori" href="#dasar-teori"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Dalam Single Linked List, setiap node menyimpan data dan pointer yang menunjuk ke node berikutnya dalam urutan sekuensial. Berikut adalah ilustrasi yang memperbaiki konsep Single Linked List:
rust
Copy code</p>
<p dir="auto">+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+
|  1  | -----&gt; |  2  | -----&gt; |  3  | -----&gt; |  4  | -----&gt; NULL
+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+
| data|        | data|        | data|        | data|
| next| -----&gt; | next| -----&gt; | next| -----&gt; | next|
+-----+        +-----+        +-----+        +-----+</p>
<p dir="auto">Pada ilustrasi di atas, terdapat empat node yang saling terhubung membentuk Single Linked List. Setiap node memiliki dua bagian utama, yaitu data (nilai yang disimpan) dan next (pointer yang menunjukkan ke node berikutnya). Node terakhir memiliki pointer next yang menunjuk ke NULL, menandakan akhir dari Single Linked List.
Node pertama memiliki data dengan nilai 1 dan next yang menunjuk ke node kedua. Node kedua memiliki data dengan nilai 2 dan next yang menunjuk ke node ketiga. Node ketiga memiliki data dengan nilai 3 dan next yang menunjuk ke node keempat. Node keempat memiliki data dengan nilai 4 dan next yang menunjuk ke NULL.
Dengan menggunakan struktur seperti ini, Single Linked List memungkinkan penyimpanan dan pengelolaan data dalam urutan sekuensial dengan fleksibilitas yang tinggi, karena node-node dapat ditambahkan atau dihapus secara dinamis.</p>
<p dir="auto">Double Linked List Circular adalah jenis dari struktur data Linked List di mana setiap node memiliki tiga bidang (field): satu bidang pointer yang menunjuk ke node berikutnya (next), satu bidang pointer yang menunjuk ke node sebelumnya (prev), dan satu bidang untuk menyimpan data yang sesuai untuk node tersebut.
Pada Double Linked List Circular, pointer next dan prev pada node terakhir di list akan menunjuk kembali ke node pertama, membentuk sebuah lingkaran atau siklus. Hal ini memungkinkan navigasi data dalam kedua arah (maju dan mundur) secara efisien dan dengan mudah, karena setiap node memiliki akses ke node sebelumnya dan node berikutnya.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Guided</h2><a id="user-content-guided" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Guided" href="#guided"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Latihan single linked list</h3><a id="user-content-1-latihan-single-linked-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Latihan single linked list" href="#1-latihan-single-linked-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &lt;iostream&gt;
using namespace std;

/// PROGRAM SINGLE LINKED LIST NON-CIRCULAR
// Deklarasi Struct Node
struct Node
{
    // komponen/member
    int data;
    Node *next;
};
Node *head;
Node *tail;
// Inisialisasi Node
void init()
{
    head = NULL;
    tail = NULL;
}
// Pengecekan
bool isEmpty()
{
    if (head == NULL)
        return true;
    else
        return false;
}
// Tambah Depan
void insertDepan(int nilai)
{
    // Buat Node baru
    Node *baru = new Node;
    baru-&gt;data = nilai;
    baru-&gt;next = NULL;
    if (isEmpty() == true)
    {
        head = tail = baru;
        tail-&gt;next = NULL;
    }
    else
    {
        baru-&gt;next = head;
        head = baru;
    }
}
// Tambah Belakang
void insertBelakang(int nilai)
{
    // Buat Node baru
    Node *baru = new Node;
    baru-&gt;data = nilai;
    baru-&gt;next = NULL;
    if (isEmpty() == true)
    {
        head = tail = baru;
        tail-&gt;next = NULL;
    }
    else
    {
        tail-&gt;next = baru;
        tail = baru;
    }
}
// Hitung Jumlah List
int hitungList()
{
    Node *hitung;
    hitung = head;
    int jumlah = 0;
    while (hitung != NULL)
    {
        jumlah++;
        hitung = hitung-&gt;next;
    }
    return jumlah;
}
// Tambah Tengah
void insertTengah(int data, int posisi)
{
    if (posisi &lt; 1 || posisi &gt; hitungList())
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi diluar jangkauan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    else if (posisi == 1)
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    else
    {
        Node *baru, *bantu;
        baru = new Node();
        baru-&gt;data = data;
        // tranversing
        bantu = head;
        int nomor = 1;
        while (nomor &lt; posisi - 1)
        {
            bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
            nomor++;
        }
        baru-&gt;next = bantu-&gt;next;
        bantu-&gt;next = baru;
    }
}
// Hapus Depan
void hapusDepan()
{
    Node *hapus;
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        if (head-&gt;next != NULL)
        {
            hapus = head;
            head = head-&gt;next;
            delete hapus;
        }
        else
        {
            head = tail = NULL;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
// Hapus Belakang
void hapusBelakang()
{
    Node *hapus;
    Node *bantu;
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        if (head != tail)
        {
            hapus = tail;
            bantu = head;
            while (bantu-&gt;next != tail)
            {
                bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
            }
            tail = bantu;
            tail-&gt;next = NULL;
            delete hapus;
        }
        else
        {
            head = tail = NULL;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
// Hapus Tengah
void hapusTengah(int posisi)
{
    Node *hapus, *bantu, *bantu2;
    if (posisi &lt; 1 || posisi &gt; hitungList())
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi di luar jangkauan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    else if (posisi == 1)
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    else
    {
        int nomor = 1;
        bantu = head;
        while (nomor &lt;= posisi)
        {
            if (nomor == posisi - 1)
            {
                bantu2 = bantu;
            }
            if (nomor == posisi)
            {
                hapus = bantu;
            }
            bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
            nomor++;
        }
        bantu2-&gt;next = bantu;
        delete hapus;
    }
}
// Ubah Depan
void ubahDepan(int data)
{
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        head-&gt;data = data;
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List masih kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
// Ubah Tengah
void ubahTengah(int data, int posisi)
{
    Node *bantu;
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        if (posisi &lt; 1 || posisi &gt; hitungList())
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi di luar jangkauan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        }
        else if (posisi == 1)
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi bukan posisi tengah&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        }
        else
        {
            bantu = head;
            int nomor = 1;
            while (nomor &lt; posisi)
            {
                bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
                nomor++;
            }
            bantu-&gt;data = data;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List masih kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
// Ubah Belakang
void ubahBelakang(int data)
{
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        tail-&gt;data = data;
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List masih kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
// Hapus List
void clearList()
{
    Node *bantu, *hapus;
    bantu = head;
    while (bantu != NULL)
    {
        hapus = bantu;
        bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
        delete hapus;
    }
    head = tail = NULL;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List berhasil terhapus!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
}
// Tampilkan List
void tampil()
{
    Node *bantu;
    bantu = head;
    if (isEmpty() == false)
    {
        while (bantu != NULL)
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; bantu-&gt;data &lt;&lt; ends;
            bantu = bantu-&gt;next;
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    else
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;List masih kosong!&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
int main()
{
    init();
    insertDepan(3);
    tampil();
    insertBelakang(5);
    tampil();
    insertDepan(2);
    tampil();
    insertDepan(1);
    tampil();
    hapusDepan();
    tampil();    hapusBelakang();
    tampil();
    insertTengah(7, 2);
    tampil();
    hapusTengah(2);
    tampil();
    ubahDepan(1);
    tampil();
    ubahBelakang(8);
    tampil();
    ubahTengah(11, 2);
    tampil();
    return 0;
}
"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>/ PROGRAM SINGLE LINKED LIST NON-CIRCULAR</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Deklarasi Struct Node</span>

{
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> komponen/member</span>
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> data;
    Node *next;
};
Node *head;
Node *tail;
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Inisialisasi Node</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">init</span>()
{
    head = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    tail = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Pengecekan</span>
<span class="pl-k">bool</span> <span class="pl-en">isEmpty</span>()
{
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head == <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Depan</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertDepan</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> nilai)
{
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Buat Node baru</span>
    Node *baru = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
    baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = nilai;
    baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">true</span>)
    {
        head = tail = baru;
        tail-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = head;
        head = baru;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Belakang</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> nilai)
{
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Buat Node baru</span>
    Node *baru = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
    baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = nilai;
    baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">true</span>)
    {
        head = tail = baru;
        tail-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        tail-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = baru;
        tail = baru;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hitung Jumlah List</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">hitungList</span>()
{
    Node *hitung;
    hitung = head;
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> jumlah = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (hitung != <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)
    {
        jumlah++;
        hitung = hitung-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> jumlah;
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Tengah</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertTengah</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> data, <span class="pl-k">int</span> posisi)
{
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi &lt; <span class="pl-c1">1</span> || posisi &gt; <span class="pl-c1">hitungList</span>())
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi diluar jangkauan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi == <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi bukan posisi tengah<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        Node *baru, *bantu;
        baru = <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">Node</span>();
        baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = data;
        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> tranversing</span>
        bantu = head;
        <span class="pl-k">int</span> nomor = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (nomor &lt; posisi - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
        {
            bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            nomor++;
        }
        baru-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = baru;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hapus Depan</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapusDepan</span>()
{
    Node *hapus;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)
        {
            hapus = head;
            head = head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">delete</span> hapus;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        {
            head = tail = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
        }
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hapus Belakang</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapusBelakang</span>()
{
    Node *hapus;
    Node *bantu;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head != tail)
        {
            hapus = tail;
            bantu = head;
            <span class="pl-k">while</span> (bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != tail)
            {
                bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            }
            tail = bantu;
            tail-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">delete</span> hapus;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        {
            head = tail = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
        }
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hapus Tengah</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapusTengah</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> posisi)
{
    Node *hapus, *bantu, *bantu2;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi &lt; <span class="pl-c1">1</span> || posisi &gt; <span class="pl-c1">hitungList</span>())
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi di luar jangkauan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi == <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi bukan posisi tengah<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        <span class="pl-k">int</span> nomor = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
        bantu = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (nomor &lt;= posisi)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (nomor == posisi - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
            {
                bantu2 = bantu;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (nomor == posisi)
            {
                hapus = bantu;
            }
            bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            nomor++;
        }
        bantu2-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = bantu;
        <span class="pl-k">delete</span> hapus;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Ubah Depan</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">ubahDepan</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> data)
{
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = data;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List masih kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Ubah Tengah</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">ubahTengah</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> data, <span class="pl-k">int</span> posisi)
{
    Node *bantu;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi &lt; <span class="pl-c1">1</span> || posisi &gt; <span class="pl-c1">hitungList</span>())
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi di luar jangkauan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (posisi == <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi bukan posisi tengah<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">else</span>
        {
            bantu = head;
            <span class="pl-k">int</span> nomor = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">while</span> (nomor &lt; posisi)
            {
                bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
                nomor++;
            }
            bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = data;
        }
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List masih kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Ubah Belakang</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">ubahBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> data)
{
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        tail-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = data;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List masih kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hapus List</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">clearList</span>()
{
    Node *bantu, *hapus;
    bantu = head;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (bantu != <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)
    {
        hapus = bantu;
        bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">delete</span> hapus;
    }
    head = tail = <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List berhasil terhapus!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tampilkan List</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">tampil</span>()
{
    Node *bantu;
    bantu = head;
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>() == <span class="pl-c1">false</span>)
    {
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (bantu != <span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>)
        {
            cout &lt;&lt; bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> &lt;&lt; ends;
            bantu = bantu-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>
    {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>List masih kosong!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}
<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>()
{
    <span class="pl-c1">init</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">insertDepan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">insertDepan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">insertDepan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">hapusDepan</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();    <span class="pl-c1">hapusBelakang</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">insertTengah</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">hapusTengah</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">ubahDepan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">ubahBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-c1">ubahTengah</span>(<span class="pl-c1">11</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">tampil</span>();
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}
</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Fungsi-fungsi ini memungkinkan pengguna untuk mengelola linked list sesuai dengan kebutuhan, baik itu menambahkan, menghapus, mengubah data, atau membersihkan seluruh isi list. Program juga memberikan feedback kepada pengguna jika terjadi kesalahan seperti menambahkan node di posisi yang tidak valid atau mengubah node yang tidak ada. Program berjalan secara interaktif, memberikan menu pilihan kepada pengguna untuk memilih operasi yang ingin dilakukan pada linked list.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Latihan double linked list</h3><a id="user-content-2-latihan-double-linked-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Latihan double linked list" href="#2-latihan-double-linked-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &lt;iostream&gt;
using namespace std;


class Node {
    public:int data;
    Node* prev;
    Node* next;
};
class DoublyLinkedList {
        public:
        Node* head;
        Node* tail;
        DoublyLinkedList() {
            head = nullptr;
            tail = nullptr;
    }
    void push(int data) {
        Node* newNode = new Node;
        newNode-&gt;data = data;
        newNode-&gt;prev = nullptr;
        newNode-&gt;next = head;
        if (head != nullptr) {
            head-&gt;prev = newNode;
        } 
        else {
            tail = newNode;
        }
        head = newNode;
    }
    void pop() {
        if (head == nullptr) {
            return;
        }
        Node* temp = head;
        head = head-&gt;next;
        if (head != nullptr) {
            head-&gt;prev = nullptr;
        } 
        else {
            tail = nullptr;
        }
        delete temp;
    }
    bool update(int oldData, int newData) {
        Node* current = head;while (current != nullptr) {
            if (current-&gt;data == oldData) {
                current-&gt;data = newData;
                return true;
            }
            current = current-&gt;next;
        }
        return false;
    }
    void deleteAll() {
        Node* current = head;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            Node* temp = current;
            current = current-&gt;next;
            delete temp;
        }
        head = nullptr;
        tail = nullptr;
    }
    void display() {
        Node* current = head;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;data &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot;;
            current = current-&gt;next;
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
};


int main() {
    DoublyLinkedList list;
    while (true) {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;1. Add data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;2. Delete data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;3. Update data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;4. Clear data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;5. Display data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;6. Exit&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;int choice;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Enter your choice: &quot;;
        cin &gt;&gt; choice;
        switch (choice) {
            case 1: {
                int data;
                cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Enter data to add: &quot;;
                cin &gt;&gt; data;
                list.push(data);
                break;
            }
            case 2: {
                list.pop();
                break;
            }
            case 3: {
                int oldData, newData;
                cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Enter old data: &quot;;
                cin &gt;&gt; oldData;
                cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Enter new data: &quot;;
                cin &gt;&gt; newData;
                bool updated = list.update(oldData, newData);
                if (!updated) {
                    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Data not found&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
                }
                break;
            }
            case 4: {
                list.deleteAll();
                break;
            }
            case 5: {
                list.display();
                break;
            }
            case 6: {
                return 0;
            }
            default: {
                cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Invalid choice&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    return 0;
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>


<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Node</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">public:</span><span class="pl-k">int</span> data;
    Node* prev;
    Node* next;
};
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">DoublyLinkedList</span> {
        <span class="pl-k">public:</span>
        Node* head;
        Node* tail;
        <span class="pl-en">DoublyLinkedList</span>() {
            head = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
            tail = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">push</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> data) {
        Node* newNode = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
        newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = data;
        newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
        newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = head;
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = newNode;
        } 
        <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
            tail = newNode;
        }
        head = newNode;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">pop</span>() {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
        }
        Node* temp = head;
        head = head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
        } 
        <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
            tail = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">delete</span> temp;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">bool</span> <span class="pl-en">update</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> oldData, <span class="pl-k">int</span> newData) {
        Node* current = head;<span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> == oldData) {
                current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> = newData;
                <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
            }
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">deleteAll</span>() {
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            Node* temp = current;
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">delete</span> temp;
        }
        head = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
        tail = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">display</span>() {
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">data</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
};


<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    DoublyLinkedList list;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (<span class="pl-c1">true</span>) {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1. Add data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2. Delete data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3. Update data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4. Clear data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5. Display data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>6. Exit<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;<span class="pl-k">int</span> choice;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Enter your choice: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
        cin &gt;&gt; choice;
        <span class="pl-k">switch</span> (choice) {
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>: {
                <span class="pl-k">int</span> data;
                cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Enter data to add: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
                cin &gt;&gt; data;
                list.<span class="pl-c1">push</span>(data);
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>: {
                list.<span class="pl-c1">pop</span>();
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>: {
                <span class="pl-k">int</span> oldData, newData;
                cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Enter old data: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
                cin &gt;&gt; oldData;
                cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Enter new data: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
                cin &gt;&gt; newData;
                <span class="pl-k">bool</span> updated = list.<span class="pl-c1">update</span>(oldData, newData);
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (!updated) {
                    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Data not found<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
                }
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span>: {
                list.<span class="pl-c1">deleteAll</span>();
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>: {
                list.<span class="pl-c1">display</span>();
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">6</span>: {
                <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">default</span>: {
                cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Invalid choice<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
                <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Kode yang Anda berikan adalah implementasi dari sebuah program yang menggunakan Double Linked List untuk mengelola data. Program ini memberikan menu interaktif kepada pengguna untuk melakukan operasi-operasi dasar pada Double Linked List, seperti menambah data, menghapus data, mengubah data, membersihkan seluruh data, dan menampilkan data.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Unguided</h2><a id="user-content-unguided" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Unguided" href="#unguided"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Soal mengenai Single Linked List</h3><a id="user-content-1-soal-mengenai-single-linked-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Soal mengenai Single Linked List" href="#1-soal-mengenai-single-linked-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Buatlah program menu Single Linked List Non-Circular untuk menyimpan Nama dan usia mahasiswa, dengan menggunakan inputan dari user. Lakukan operasi berikut:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &lt;iostream&gt;
#include &lt;string&gt;
using namespace std;

// Deklarasi Struct Node
struct Node {
    string nama;
    int usia;
    Node* next;
};

// Inisialisasi Node
Node* head = nullptr;

// Pengecekan List Kosong
bool isEmpty() {
    return head == nullptr;
}

// Tambah Node di Depan
void insertDepan(string nama, int usia) {
    Node* newNode = new Node;
    newNode-&gt;nama = nama;
    newNode-&gt;usia = usia;
    newNode-&gt;next = head;
    head = newNode;
}

// Tambah Node di Belakang
void insertBelakang(string nama, int usia) {
    Node* newNode = new Node;
    newNode-&gt;nama = nama;
    newNode-&gt;usia = usia;
    newNode-&gt;next = nullptr;
    
    if (isEmpty()) {
        head = newNode;
        return;
    }

    Node* current = head;
    while (current-&gt;next != nullptr) {
        current = current-&gt;next;
    }
    current-&gt;next = newNode;
}

// Tambah Node di Tengah
void insertTengah(string nama, int usia, string posisi) {
    Node* current = head;
    while (current != nullptr &amp;&amp; current-&gt;nama != posisi) {
        current = current-&gt;next;
    }

    if (current == nullptr) {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Posisi tidak ditemukan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        return;
    }

    Node* newNode = new Node;
    newNode-&gt;nama = nama;
    newNode-&gt;usia = usia;
    newNode-&gt;next = current-&gt;next;
    current-&gt;next = newNode;
}

// Hapus Node dengan Nama Tertentu
void hapus(string targetNama) {
    Node* current = head;
    Node* prev = nullptr;

    while (current != nullptr &amp;&amp; current-&gt;nama != targetNama) {
        prev = current;
        current = current-&gt;next;
    }

    if (current == nullptr) {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Data tidak ditemukan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        return;
    }

    if (prev == nullptr) {
        head = current-&gt;next;
    } else {
        prev-&gt;next = current-&gt;next;
    }

    delete current;
}

// Ubah Data Node dengan Nama Tertentu
void ubahData(string targetNama, string newNama, int newUsia) {
    Node* current = head;
    while (current != nullptr &amp;&amp; current-&gt;nama != targetNama) {
        current = current-&gt;next;
    }
    if (current != nullptr) {
        current-&gt;nama = newNama;
        current-&gt;usia = newUsia;
    } else {
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Data tidak ditemukan&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}

// Tampilkan Seluruh Data
void tampilkanData() {
    Node* current = head;
    while (current != nullptr) {
        cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;nama &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot; &lt;&lt; current-&gt;usia &lt;&lt; endl;
        current = current-&gt;next;
    }
}

int main() {
    string namaAnda;
    int usiaAnda;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Masukkan Nama Anda: &quot;;
    cin &gt;&gt; namaAnda;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Masukkan Usia Anda: &quot;;
    cin &gt;&gt; usiaAnda;

    insertDepan(namaAnda, usiaAnda);

    insertBelakang(&quot;John&quot;, 19);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Jane&quot;, 20);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Michael&quot;, 18);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Yusuke&quot;, 19);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Akechi&quot;, 20);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Hoshino&quot;, 18);
    insertBelakang(&quot;Karin&quot;, 18);

    hapus(&quot;Akechi&quot;);
    insertTengah(&quot;Futaba&quot;, 18, &quot;John&quot;);
    insertDepan(&quot;Igor&quot;, 20);
    ubahData(&quot;Michael&quot;, &quot;Reyn&quot;, 18);

    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Data Mahasiswa:&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    tampilkanData();

    return 0;
}

"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>string<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Deklarasi Struct Node</span>
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">Node</span> {
    string nama;
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> usia;
    Node* next;
};

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Inisialisasi Node</span>
Node* head = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Pengecekan List Kosong</span>
<span class="pl-k">bool</span> <span class="pl-en">isEmpty</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> head == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Node di Depan</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertDepan</span>(string nama, <span class="pl-k">int</span> usia) {
    Node* newNode = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> = nama;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">usia</span> = usia;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = head;
    head = newNode;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Node di Belakang</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertBelakang</span>(string nama, <span class="pl-k">int</span> usia) {
    Node* newNode = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> = nama;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">usia</span> = usia;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">isEmpty</span>()) {
        head = newNode;
        <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
    }

    Node* current = head;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }
    current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = newNode;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tambah Node di Tengah</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">insertTengah</span>(string nama, <span class="pl-k">int</span> usia, string posisi) {
    Node* current = head;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> != posisi) {
        current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Posisi tidak ditemukan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
    }

    Node* newNode = <span class="pl-k">new</span> Node;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> = nama;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">usia</span> = usia;
    newNode-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = newNode;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Hapus Node dengan Nama Tertentu</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapus</span>(string targetNama) {
    Node* current = head;
    Node* prev = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;

    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> != targetNama) {
        prev = current;
        current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Data tidak ditemukan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (prev == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        head = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
        prev-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">delete</span> current;
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Ubah Data Node dengan Nama Tertentu</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">ubahData</span>(string targetNama, string newNama, <span class="pl-k">int</span> newUsia) {
    Node* current = head;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> != targetNama) {
        current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> = newNama;
        current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">usia</span> = newUsia;
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Data tidak ditemukan<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tampilkan Seluruh Data</span>
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">tampilkanData</span>() {
    Node* current = head;
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
        cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">usia</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
    }
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    string namaAnda;
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> usiaAnda;

    <span class="pl-c1">insertDepan</span>(namaAnda, usiaAnda);

    <span class="pl-c1">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>John<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">19</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Jane<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Michael<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">18</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">insertBelakang</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Yusuke<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">19</span>);
