<p dir="auto">Program yang Anda berikan adalah implementasi dari Single Linked List Non-Circular dalam bahasa C++. Program ini menyediakan fungsi-fungsi dasar untuk mengelola linked list, seperti menambahkan node di depan, belakang, atau tengah, menghapus node dengan nama tertentu, mengubah data node, dan menampilkan seluruh data yang tersimpan dalam linked list.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ss kode</h2><a id="user-content-ss-kode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ss kode" href="#ss-kode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317350223-9ce7601c-e8d1-4ade-ae0f-43e3059e3cee.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzUwMjIzLTljZTc2MDFjLWU4ZDEtNGFkZS1hZTBmLTQzZTMwNTllM2NlZS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT04MzZkMWY4ZWY1MGVmNWIzZTliOTI4NjVkNmYwNDdkM2IwMjM1YWI5M2IzZmNjNWJlMWUyZTI5NmE0NTZhMGY1JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.4A-9WfHG1V1gM5bf0xQak53n6RFrlpdh5qGX-smxExY"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317350223-9ce7601c-e8d1-4ade-ae0f-43e3059e3cee.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzUwMjIzLTljZTc2MDFjLWU4ZDEtNGFkZS1hZTBmLTQzZTMwNTllM2NlZS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT04MzZkMWY4ZWY1MGVmNWIzZTliOTI4NjVkNmYwNDdkM2IwMjM1YWI5M2IzZmNjNWJlMWUyZTI5NmE0NTZhMGY1JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.4A-9WfHG1V1gM5bf0xQak53n6RFrlpdh5qGX-smxExY" alt="Screenshot (152)" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Kesimpulan dari Materi single linked list :</h2><a id="user-content-kesimpulan-dari-materi-single-linked-list-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Kesimpulan dari Materi single linked list :" href="#kesimpulan-dari-materi-single-linked-list-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Dengan memahami konsep dan operasi pada single linked list, seseorang dapat lebih efektif dalam merancang, mengimplementasikan, dan memanfaatkan struktur data ini dalam pemrograman dan pengembangan perangkat lunak secara umum.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Soal mengenai Double Linked List</h3><a id="user-content-2-soal-mengenai-double-linked-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Soal mengenai Double Linked List" href="#2-soal-mengenai-double-linked-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Modifikasi Guided Double Linked List dilakukan dengan penambahan operasi untuk menambah data, menghapus, dan update di tengah / di urutan tertentu yang diminta. Selain itu, buatlah agar tampilannya menampilkan Nama produk dan harga
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317353292-6d155755-4ed5-4e75-a438-d59df7af228d.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzUzMjkyLTZkMTU1NzU1LTRlZDUtNGU3NS1hNDM4LWQ1OWRmN2FmMjI4ZC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0zMjJiMTNlZjUxNGI0ZTUxMDBiYjFmNDBlN2UxZjkwNjMyYzllMzFmZTU3NDlmZDIxM2ZkZGE0NjEzYTBmM2Q5JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.GFnSuuSHSkcoR0vQtSjdDmca7nlHq6858kbb9gJEM7E"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317353292-6d155755-4ed5-4e75-a438-d59df7af228d.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzUzMjkyLTZkMTU1NzU1LTRlZDUtNGU3NS1hNDM4LWQ1OWRmN2FmMjI4ZC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0zMjJiMTNlZjUxNGI0ZTUxMDBiYjFmNDBlN2UxZjkwNjMyYzllMzFmZTU3NDlmZDIxM2ZkZGE0NjEzYTBmM2Q5JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.GFnSuuSHSkcoR0vQtSjdDmca7nlHq6858kbb9gJEM7E" alt="Screenshot 2024-03-27 232425" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#include &lt;iostream&gt;
#include &lt;string&gt;
using namespace std;

class Node {
public:
    string nama_produk;
    int harga;
    Node* next;
    Node* prev;

    Node(string nama_produk, int harga) {
        this-&gt;nama_produk = nama_produk;
        this-&gt;harga = harga;
        this-&gt;next = nullptr;
        this-&gt;prev = nullptr;
    }
};

class DoublyLinkedList {
private:
    Node* head;

public:
    DoublyLinkedList() {
        head = nullptr;
    }

    void tambah_data(string nama_produk, int harga) {
        Node* new_node = new Node(nama_produk, harga);
        if (head == nullptr) {
            head = new_node;
        } else {
            Node* current = head;
            while (current-&gt;next != nullptr) {
                current = current-&gt;next;
            }
            current-&gt;next = new_node;
            new_node-&gt;prev = current;
        }
    }

    void hapus_data(string nama_produk) {
        Node* current = head;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            if (current-&gt;nama_produk == nama_produk) {
                if (current-&gt;prev != nullptr) {
                    current-&gt;prev-&gt;next = current-&gt;next;
                }
                if (current-&gt;next != nullptr) {
                    current-&gt;next-&gt;prev = current-&gt;prev;
                }
                if (current == head) {
                    head = current-&gt;next;
                }
                delete current;
                return;
            }
            current = current-&gt;next;
        }
    }

    void update_data(string nama_produk, int harga) {
        Node* current = head;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            if (current-&gt;nama_produk == nama_produk) {
                current-&gt;harga = harga;
                return;
            }
            current = current-&gt;next;
        }
    }

    void tambah_data_urutan_tertentu(string nama_produk, int harga, int urutan) {
        Node* new_node = new Node(nama_produk, harga);
        if (urutan == 1 || head == nullptr) {
            new_node-&gt;next = head;
            if (head != nullptr) {
                head-&gt;prev = new_node;
            }
            head = new_node;
        } else {
            Node* current = head;
            int count = 1;
            while (current != nullptr &amp;&amp; count &lt; urutan - 1) {
                current = current-&gt;next;
                count++;
            }
            if (current == nullptr) {
                cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Urutan melebihi jumlah produk yang ada&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
                return;
            }
            new_node-&gt;next = current-&gt;next;
            new_node-&gt;prev = current;
            if (current-&gt;next != nullptr) {
                current-&gt;next-&gt;prev = new_node;
            }
            current-&gt;next = new_node;
        }
    }

    void hapus_data_urutan_tertentu(int urutan) {
        if (head == nullptr) {
            return;
        }
        Node* current = head;
        if (urutan == 1) {
            head = current-&gt;next;
            if (head != nullptr) {
                head-&gt;prev = nullptr;
            }
            delete current;
            return;
        }
        int count = 1;
        while (current != nullptr &amp;&amp; count &lt; urutan) {
            current = current-&gt;next;
            count++;
        }
        if (current == nullptr) {
            return;
        }
        if (current-&gt;next != nullptr) {
            current-&gt;next-&gt;prev = current-&gt;prev;
        }
        if (current-&gt;prev != nullptr) {
            current-&gt;prev-&gt;next = current-&gt;next;
        }
        delete current;
    }

    void hapus_seluruh_data() {
        Node* current = head;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            Node* next_node = current-&gt;next;
            delete current;
            current = next_node;
        }
        head = nullptr;
    }

    void tampilkan_data() {
        Node* current = head;
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Nama Produk Harga&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
        while (current != nullptr) {
            cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;nama_produk &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot; &lt;&lt; current-&gt;harga &lt;&lt; endl;
            current = current-&gt;next;
        }
    }
};

int main() {
    DoublyLinkedList dll;

    // Menambahkan data awal
    dll.tambah_data(&quot;Originote&quot;, 60000);
    dll.tambah_data(&quot;Somethinc&quot;, 150000);
    dll.tambah_data(&quot;Skintific&quot;, 100000);
    dll.tambah_data(&quot;Wardah&quot;, 50000);
    dll.tambah_data(&quot;Hanasui&quot;, 30000);

    // Modifikasi sesuai dengan case yang diberikan
    dll.tambah_data_urutan_tertentu(&quot;Azarine&quot;, 65000, 3);
    dll.hapus_data(&quot;Wardah&quot;);
    dll.update_data(&quot;Hanasui&quot;, 55000);

    // Tampilkan menu
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Toko Skincare Purwokerto&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;1. Tambah Data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;2. Hapus Data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;3. Update Data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;4. Tambah Data Urutan Tertentu&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;5. Hapus Data Urutan Tertentu&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;6. Hapus Seluruh Data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;7. Tampilkan Data&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; &quot;8. Exit&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;

    // Tampilkan data setelah modifikasi
    dll.tampilkan_data();

    return 0;
}"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>string<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">std</span><span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Node</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
    string nama_produk;
    <span class="pl-k">int</span> harga;
    Node* next;
    Node* prev;

    <span class="pl-en">Node</span>(string nama_produk, <span class="pl-k">int</span> harga) {
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama_produk</span> = nama_produk;
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">harga</span> = harga;
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    }
};

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">DoublyLinkedList</span> {
<span class="pl-k">private:</span>
    Node* head;

<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
    <span class="pl-en">DoublyLinkedList</span>() {
        head = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">tambah_data</span>(string nama_produk, <span class="pl-k">int</span> harga) {
        Node* new_node = <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">Node</span>(nama_produk, harga);
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            head = new_node;
        } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
            Node* current = head;
            <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            }
            current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = new_node;
            new_node-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = current;
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapus_data</span>(string nama_produk) {
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama_produk</span> == nama_produk) {
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                    current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
                }
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                    current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span>;
                }
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current == head) {
                    head = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
                }
                <span class="pl-k">delete</span> current;
                <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
            }
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">update_data</span>(string nama_produk, <span class="pl-k">int</span> harga) {
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama_produk</span> == nama_produk) {
                current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">harga</span> = harga;
                <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
            }
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">tambah_data_urutan_tertentu</span>(string nama_produk, <span class="pl-k">int</span> harga, <span class="pl-k">int</span> urutan) {
        Node* new_node = <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">Node</span>(nama_produk, harga);
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (urutan == <span class="pl-c1">1</span> || head == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            new_node-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = head;
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = new_node;
            }
            head = new_node;
        } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
            Node* current = head;
            <span class="pl-k">int</span> count = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; count &lt; urutan - <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) {
                current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
                count++;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Urutan melebihi jumlah produk yang ada<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
                <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
            }
            new_node-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            new_node-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = current;
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = new_node;
            }
            current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = new_node;
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapus_data_urutan_tertentu</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> urutan) {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
        }
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (urutan == <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) {
            head = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (head != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
                head-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
            }
            <span class="pl-k">delete</span> current;
            <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">int</span> count = <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; count &lt; urutan) {
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            count++;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current == <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span> != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">prev</span>-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span> = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
        <span class="pl-k">delete</span> current;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">hapus_seluruh_data</span>() {
        Node* current = head;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            Node* next_node = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">delete</span> current;
            current = next_node;
        }
        head = <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">tampilkan_data</span>() {
        Node* current = head;
        cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Nama Produk Harga<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        <span class="pl-k">while</span> (current != <span class="pl-c1">nullptr</span>) {
            cout &lt;&lt; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">nama_produk</span> &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">harga</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
            current = current-&gt;<span class="pl-smi">next</span>;
        }
    }
};

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    DoublyLinkedList dll;

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Menambahkan data awal</span>
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Originote<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">60000</span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Somethinc<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">150000</span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Skintific<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">100000</span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Wardah<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">50000</span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hanasui<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">30000</span>);

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Modifikasi sesuai dengan case yang diberikan</span>
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tambah_data_urutan_tertentu</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Azarine<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">65000</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">hapus_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Wardah<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">update_data</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hanasui<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">55000</span>);

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tampilkan menu</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Toko Skincare Purwokerto<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1. Tambah Data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2. Hapus Data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3. Update Data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4. Tambah Data Urutan Tertentu<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5. Hapus Data Urutan Tertentu<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>6. Hapus Seluruh Data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>7. Tampilkan Data<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>8. Exit<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Tampilkan data setelah modifikasi</span>
    dll.<span class="pl-c1">tampilkan_data</span>();

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Output:</h4><a id="user-content-output-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Output:" href="#output-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto">Program yang Anda berikan adalah implementasi dari doubly linked list untuk menyimpan data produk skincare beserta harganya. Program ini memiliki beberapa fungsi utama seperti tambah data, hapus data, update data, tambah data pada urutan tertentu, hapus data pada urutan tertentu, hapus seluruh data, dan menampilkan data.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317365862-f8477d2a-9889-40ba-a26f-9989a1775478.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzY1ODYyLWY4NDc3ZDJhLTk4ODktNDBiYS1hMjZmLTk5ODlhMTc3NTQ3OC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0zMTEwZjg3NDI2NGIyMmMxYjAzMjM5NTliZTlkNjQ0NTkyYWYzOGNiM2NlNzZhMzEyMjgxZTY1ODg3NDEyMmJjJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.ORn0mZkKBXDoiZ7dqK216e6UkG15QsOEUPS0Xwi4xK4"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/162522335/317365862-f8477d2a-9889-40ba-a26f-9989a1775478.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MTE1NjEyMTAsIm5iZiI6MTcxMTU2MDkxMCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNjI1MjIzMzUvMzE3MzY1ODYyLWY4NDc3ZDJhLTk4ODktNDBiYS1hMjZmLTk5ODlhMTc3NTQ3OC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMzI3JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDMyN1QxNzM1MTBaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0zMTEwZjg3NDI2NGIyMmMxYjAzMjM5NTliZTlkNjQ0NTkyYWYzOGNiM2NlNzZhMzEyMjgxZTY1ODg3NDEyMmJjJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.ORn0mZkKBXDoiZ7dqK216e6UkG15QsOEUPS0Xwi4xK4" alt="Screenshot (118)" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Program yang Anda berikan merupakan implementasi dari doubly linked list untuk menyimpan data produk skincare beserta harga. Program ini juga memiliki fungsi-fungsi tambah, hapus, update, tambah urutan tertentu, hapus urutan tertentu, dan hapus seluruh data.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Referensi</h2><a id="user-content-referensi" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Referensi" href="#referensi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
